# CartFlow вЂ” System Summary (Architecture)

## 1) System Overview

CartFlow is a FastAPI application that:

- Embeds a storefront **widget** (JavaScript) for hesitation / exit-intent UX and **reason capture**.
- Receives **cart lifecycle events** (e.g. abandon, conversion) via **`POST /api/cart-event`** and schedules **delayed WhatsApp recovery** (Twilio path in `services/whatsapp_send.py`; Meta Cloud API path in `main.send_whatsapp_message` for interactive CTA messages used elsewhere).
- Persists **store settings**, **abandoned carts**, **recovery reasons**, and **recovery logs** in SQLAlchemy models (`models.py`), with optional schema patches via `schema_widget.py`.
- Serves **merchant dashboards** as Jinja2 HTML under `/dashboard/*`, loading/saving settings through **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`** and related APIs.
- **`GET /`** вЂ” public marketing landing (`templates/cartflow_landing.html`): Arabic RTL **product-story landing** вЂ” behavior + objection + recovery + explanation (hero flow, real dashboard screenshots for objection reasons / recovery templates / carts / widget / WhatsApp); no fake ROI; CTAs **`/signup`** and **`/login`**.

### 1.1 Commercial packaging (approved foundation вЂ” audit only, no billing)

| Package | Monthly (SAR) | Annual (SAR) | Target merchant |
|---------|---------------|--------------|-----------------|
| **Starter** | 99 | 990 | Entry вЂ” widget, reason capture, single-path WhatsApp recovery, dashboard, basic analytics, default templates |
| **Growth** (Most Popular) | 199 | 1,990 | Active stores вЂ” adds VIP detection/alerts, multi-message, per-reason templates/timing, advanced analytics, merchant controls |
| **Pro** | 399 | 3,990 | High maturity вЂ” advanced recovery/message logic, operational insights, early access, future intelligence modules |

**Pricing model:** feature-based; monthly + annual; **no message/recovery quotas** in marketing (internal fair usage may apply later). Pricing audit: **`docs/cartflow_packages_pricing_foundation_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 1 (implemented вЂ” no payment processing):** canonical plans + entitlements (`services/cartflow_plans_v1.py`, `services/cartflow_entitlements_v1.py`); subscription state on **`MerchantUser`** (`current_plan`, `plan_status`, `plan_source`, `plan_started_at`, `plan_expires_at`); `GET /api/merchant/subscription` + read-only dashboard card; marketplace event vocabulary (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*` вЂ” architecture only). Enforcement via **`CARTFLOW_PLAN_ENTITLEMENTS_ENFORCE`** (default off). Audit: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase1_marketplace_plan_system_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 2 (pricing & subscription UI вЂ” visual only):** enhanced current-plan card on `#settings`; read-only plans comparison page `#plans` (Starter/Growth/Pro features + SAR pricing); `GET /api/merchant/plans-catalog`; `merchant_plans_ui.js`; topbar В«Ш§Щ„ШЁШ§Щ‚Ш©В» в†’ `#plans`. No upgrade/billing/checkout. Visual proof: `scripts/_saas_plans_ui_out/`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_plans_ui_v1.py`.

**SaaS foundation Phase 3 (trial & admin subscription control):** Admin `/admin/subscriptions/control` вЂ” manual plan/trial assignment, audit log, merchant dashboard reflects Trial status; no billing. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_trial_admin_subscription_control_audit_v1.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 3.1 (automatic subscription dates):** `billing_interval` (`trial` / `monthly` / `annual` / `manual_custom`); admin preset actions auto-compute dates (14 / 30 / 365 days); custom dates only for `manual_custom`; enriched audit log; merchant dashboard shows interval + trial/plan expiry; marketplace date helper (`merchant_billing_interval_v1.py`). Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase3_1_automatic_subscription_dates_audit_v1.md`**.

**Marketplace Subscription Sync v1 (architecture audit only):** Six event types (`zid_plan_*`, `salla_plan_*` including `*_cancelled`); normalized adapter contract в†’ `MerchantUser` field mapping; store linkage; idempotent receipts + audit log; admin fallback; failure taxonomy. No webhooks implemented. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_marketplace_subscription_sync_v1_audit.md`**.

**SaaS foundation Phase 4 (subscription experience):** Subscription Status Card V2 (plan/status/source badges, days remaining, health messages); current plan benefits + read-only upgrade discovery; admin list shows days remaining + health. No billing/checkout/enforcement. Doc: **`docs/cartflow_saas_foundation_phase4_subscription_experience_audit_v1.md`**.

## 2) Frontend Layer

### 2.1 Widget Layer (VERY IMPORTANT)

| Asset | Role |
|--------|------|
| `static/widget_loader.js` | Parses **`cartflowEarlyCartClickBootstrap`** at DCL (or immediately if document already interactive) вЂ” minimal capture-phase add-to-cart listener queues clicks before V2 loads; replayed by `zidCartEventSource` after bridge init. After **`window.load`**: schedules **`cartflow_return_tracker.js`**, then loads the widget. **Default storefront path:** layered **`cartflow_widget_runtime/cartflow_widget_loader.js`** (serial module chain) whenever **`window.__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET !== true`** *or* **`window.CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2 === true`** (**`loadLayeredV2 = runtimeV2Explicit \|\| !legacyExplicit`** in shim). **Legacy `cartflow_widget.js`** loads **only** when **`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET === true`** **and** **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2` is not** `true` (rollback / QA вЂ” console **`[CF LEGACY WIDGET LOAD ALLOWED]`** vs **`[CF LEGACY WIDGET LOAD BLOCKED]`**). **`/demo/store*`** sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2 = true`** in the shim (**`cartflowIsDemoStorePrimaryV2Path()`**); **`templates/demo_store.html`** also sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2`** before the shim. Merchant dashboard embed (**`general_settings.html`**) references **`widget_loader.js` only** в†’ **production default is V2**, not legacy. Skips tracker/widget bootstrap when session marked converted via `sessionStorage` / `cartflowIsSessionConverted`. Duplicate script detection skips re-injecting if runtime or legacy URL already present. |
| `static/cartflow_widget_runtime/*.js` | **Layered V2** storefront widget (config в†’ API в†’ state в†’ triggers в†’ **storefront cart bridge** в†’ cart sources в†’ cart event bridge в†’ phone в†’ shell в†’ UI в†’ flows в†’ legacy_bridge). Starts via **`Flows.start()`** after bootstrap. Does **not** append **`cartflow_widget.js`** at runtime; VIP mirrors use **`mirrorCartTotals()`** in **`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** only. |
| `static/cartflow_widget.js` | **Legacy monolith** (`B`): **not** the default shim branch вЂ” loads only with **explicit** **`window.__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET === true`** while **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2` is not** `true`, or via **`GET /dev/widget-test*`** (**`main._DEV_LEGACY_WIDGET_HARNESS_HTML`**, **`ENV=development`** only вЂ” **not** in **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`**). Retained for **rollback**, **dev harness**, and **static/operational test reads** (`tests/**` grep static file). **`/demo/store*`** does **not** load this asset in the happy path. |
| `static/cartflow_return_tracker.js` | Loaded by **`widget_loader.js`** (return-to-site / behavioral handoff signalling). |
| `static/cart_abandon_tracking.js` | Included from dashboard templates (`partials/cart_abandon_tracking.html`) for analytics-style tracking where wired. |

**Primary backend calls from storefront widgets:**

- **V2 (`cartflow_widget_fetch.js`, namespace `Api`):** `POST /api/cartflow/reason`, `GET /api/cartflow/ready`, `GET /api/cartflow/public-config` (`routes/cartflow.py`).
- **Legacy (`cartflow_widget.js`):** `POST /api/cart-recovery/reason` вЂ” persist widget **Layer D** (`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`); `POST /api/cartflow/reason` alternate path (`routes/cartflow.py`).
- Shared / either surface as wired: `GET /api/recovery/primary-reason` вЂ” `main.py`; `POST /api/cartflow/generate-whatsapp-message` вЂ” mock WhatsApp preview (no DB write in that handler).

**Cart abandon signal to backend:** the storefront integration is expected to call **`POST /api/cart-event`** with `event: cart_abandoned` (handled in `main.handle_cart_abandoned` в†’ recovery dispatch). The widget focuses on reasons and UX; the actual **abandon event** is typically from page / platform integration.

### 2.1.1 Widget architecture вЂ” operational posture (audit 2026-05)

| Topic | Assessment |
|--------|------------|
| **Default production behavior** | **Layered V2** via **`widget_loader.js`** without any global legacy opt-in (evidence: **`templates/general_settings.html`** embed = `widget_loader.js` only; shim **`loadLayeredV2`** true when **`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET` is not** set). |
| **Demo / primary V2 enforcement** | **`demo_store.html`** sets **`CARTFLOW_WIDGET_RUNTIME_V2`** + **`CARTFLOW_RUNTIME_VERSION`** before shim; shim **also** forces V2 on **`^/demo/store(/|$)`**. Baseline tests: **`tests/test_v2_widget_baseline_lock.py`**, **`tests/test_demo_behavioral_navigation.py`**. |
| **`cartflow_widget_runtime` load model** | **`cartflow_widget_loader.js`** loads modules **sequentially** (`async: false` tags, ordered **config в†’ api в†’ state в†’ arbitration в†’ theme в†’ triggers в†’ storefront cart bridge (contract/adapters/core) в†’ cart_sources в†’ cart_event_bridge в†’ phone в†’ shell в†’ ui в†’ flows в†’ legacy_bridge**), then **`__cartflowV2Bootstrap` / `Flows.start()`**. **`cartflow_widget_arbitration.js`** logs `[CF ARBITRATION *]` open intents/decisions; **Exit Intent No-Cart v1** enforces **`exit_without_cart_blocked`** via **`gateExitIntentOpen()`** on exit open paths (other journeys remain shadow observe). Failure of one module aborts the chain (logged **`[CF V2 MODULE FAILED]`**). **Storefront Cart Bridge** (`cartflow_storefront_cart_bridge_*.js`) reads platform carts via adapters (Zid first: `/api/v1/cart`, add-to-cart response, `window.cart` fallback), validates a normalized payload, dedupes, and **only the core** posts **`POST /api/cart-event`** (`cart_state_sync`) with additive **`cf_storefront_cart_bridge`** metadata. The platform-neutral **Cart Event Bridge** (`cartflow_cart_event_bridge.js`) + signal adapters (`cartflow_cart_sources.js`) still normalize platform cart **signals** into one `CartFlowCartEvent`, route them through **`Cf.Triggers.onNormalizedCartEvent`** (orchestrator decides display), and delegate persistence to **Storefront Cart Bridge** before legacy **`cartflowSyncCartState`**. Canonical merchant store resolved server-side + `canonical_store_slug` from **`public-config`**. |
| **Complexity / bundle** | V2 split across **~10** smaller files (~**118 KB** source on disk, pre-minify); legacy monolith ~**337 KB**. Default path avoids legacy download; total widget surface still **multiple HTTP round-trips** for V2 (shim + tracker + loader + 9 modules). |
| **Duplication / coupling** | **Dual** reason APIs (**`/api/cartflow/reason`** vs **`/api/cart-recovery/reason`**); **dual** exit-intent implementations (V2 modules vs legacy file); **shared** backend contract (**`exit_intent_*`**, templates). **Operational / static** tests still scan **`cartflow_widget.js`** for parity. |
| **Legacy isolation** | V2 **does not** inject legacy at runtime (**`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** / audit: no `injectLegacyCartflowWidget`). Rollback is **merchant opt-in** + dev harness only. |
| **Risk level** | **Moderate:** default is healthy (V2), but **two** storefront stacks and **serial** multi-file load remain **maintainability and performance** considerations until legacy sunset. |

### 2.2 Dashboard UI

| Path / files | Purpose |
|--------------|---------|
| `GET /dashboard` | `merchant_app.html` вЂ” **ШґШ±ЩЉШ· Ш№Щ„Щ€ЩЉ** (ШЈЩЉЩ† ШЈЩ†Ш§Шџ) + **Ш¬Ш§Щ†ШЁЩЉ ШіЩЉШ§Щ‚ЩЉ** (Щ…Ш§Ш°Ш§ ШЈЩЃШ№Щ„ Щ‡Щ†Ш§Шџ) + Щ…Ш­ШЄЩ€Щ‰ Щ€Ш§Ш­ШЇШ› lazy JSON Ш№ШЁШ± `/api/dashboard/*`. **Home section (4 sub-pages via `#home` / `#home-setup` / `#home-month` / `#home-test-tools`):** **Overview (`#home`)** вЂ” Knowledge Layer (В«Щ…Ш§Ш°Ш§ ЩЉШ­ШЇШ« ЩЃЩЉ Щ…ШЄШ¬Ш±ЩЉ Ш§Щ„ШўЩ†ШџВ»)ШЊ ШЈШіШЁШ§ШЁ Ш§Щ„ШЈШіШЁЩ€Ш№ШЊ VIP highlights вЂ” **ШЁШЇЩ€Щ†** KPIs Ш§ШіШЄШ±ШЇШ§ШЇШ› **Store Setup (`#home-setup`)** вЂ” `#ma-setup-readiness-root` + `#ma-setup-experience-root` + `#ma-activation-root`Ш› **Ш§Щ„Щ…Щ„Ш®Шµ Ш§Щ„Ш№Ш§Щ… (`#home-month`)** вЂ” `#ma-home-month-summary` (Щ…Щ„Ш®Шµ Ш§Щ„ШґЩ‡Ш±) + В«ШЈШЁШ±ШІ Ш§Щ„Ш§ШіШЄШ±ШЇШ§ШЇ вЂ” Ш§Щ„ЩЉЩ€Щ…В»Ш› **Test Tools (`#home-test-tools`)** вЂ” `#ma-test-tools-root` (`ЩЃШЄШ­ Щ…ШЄШ¬Ш± Ш§Щ„Ш§Ш®ШЄШЁШ§Ш±` в†’ `/dashboard/test-widget` ШЈЩ€ `/demo/store`Ш› `Ш№Ш±Ш¶ Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„` в†’ `#carts`). **Carts (`#carts`):** `#ma-cart-alerts-root` (Cart Alerts вЂ” VIP banner ЩЃЩ€Щ‚ `#ma-cart-filters`Ш› Щ…Ш®ЩЃЩЉ ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„ VIP). **Customer lifecycle v1:** normal-carts rows expose `customer_lifecycle_*` (8 states, Arabic labels, explanation block) via `services/customer_lifecycle_states_v1.py`; status column uses lifecycle label (not legacy static copy alone). **Archive:** `POST /api/dashboard/cart-lifecycle/archive` + `/reopen` в†’ `merchant_cart_lifecycle_archive` (`services/merchant_cart_lifecycle_archive_v1.py`); writes all canonical `recovery_key` aliases. **`GET /api/dashboard/normal-carts`** returns `merchant_archived_carts_page_rows` (`lifecycle=archived`); ШЄШЁЩ€ЩЉШЁ **Щ…ЩѓШЄЩ…Щ„Ш©** ЩЉШ№Ш±Ш¶ Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш¤Ш±ШґЩЃШ© + Ш§Щ„Щ…ШіШЄШ±ШЇШ© Щ…Ш№ **ШҐШ№Ш§ШЇШ© ЩЃШЄШ­**. Merchant-archived carts excluded from **active** and **all** operational lists until reopen. **VIP phone:** `vip_phone_capture` в†’ `apply_vip_phone_capture_to_abandoned_carts` (threshold lane + `vip_mode`); dashboard reads `AbandonedCart.customer_phone` first. |
| `GET /dashboard/recovery-settings` | `recovery_settings.html` вЂ” delay, attempts, WhatsApp fields; **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard#whatsapp` | `merchant_app.html` вЂ” **ШЄШ¬Ш±ШЁШ© Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁ V3:** Ш§Ш®ШЄЩЉШ§Ш± Ш§Щ„Щ…ШіШ§Ш± (CartFlow / Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁ ШЈШ№Щ…Ш§Щ„ЩЉ)ШЊ ШЁШ·Ш§Щ‚Ш© В«Ш§Щ„Щ…ШіШ§Ш± Ш§Щ„Ш­Ш§Щ„ЩЉВ»ШЊ ШҐШ№ШЇШ§ШЇШ§ШЄ Щ…ШЄЩ‚ШЇЩ…Ш© (merchant ЩЃЩ‚Ш·). **`#whatsapp-connect`** вЂ” ШµЩЃШ­Ш© Ш±ШЁШ· ШЄШ¬Ш§Ш±ЩЉШ© (Щ„ЩЉШі ШЄЩ‚Щ†ЩЉШ©). **`GET`/`POST /api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard#plans` | `merchant_app.html` вЂ” **read-only plans comparison** (Starter/Growth/Pro features + SAR pricing; Growth = Most Popular); current plan summary; **`GET /api/merchant/plans-catalog`**. No upgrade/billing. |
| `GET /dashboard#settings` | `merchant_app.html` вЂ” store connection + general settings + **read-only current plan card** (`GET /api/merchant/subscription`). |
| `GET /dashboard#vip` | `merchant_app.html` вЂ” VIP preferences (enable, threshold, notify toggle, note) + existing VIP cart table; **`/api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings` | `vip_cart_settings.html` вЂ” **ШЈЩ€Щ„Щ€ЩЉШ© Ш­Щ‚ЩЉЩ‚ЩЉШ©:** `AbandonedCart.status=abandoned` Щ€вЂЋ`coalesce(cart_value,0) >= Store.vip_cart_threshold` Ш№Щ†ШЇ ШЄШ№Ш±ЩЉЩЃ Ш§Щ„Ш№ШЄШЁШ©Ш› ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† Ш№ШЄШЁШ© Щ„Ш§ ШЄЩЏШ№Ш±Ш¶ Щ‚Ш§Ш¦Щ…Ш© VIP. **ШЁЩЉШ§Щ†Ш§ШЄ ШЄШ¬Ш±ЩЉШЁЩЉШ©** Щ…Щ†ЩЃШµЩ„Ш© (`interactive: false`). **ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ ЩЉШЇЩ€ЩЉ** в†’ **`POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{abandoned_cart_row_id}/merchant-alert`**. Ш№ШЄШЁШ© VIP Ш№ШЁШ± **`/api/recovery-settings`**. |
| `GET /dashboard/exit-intent-settings` | `exit_intent_settings.html` вЂ” exit intent copy; loads/saves via recovery settings API + `static/cartflow_dashboard_messages.js`. |
| `GET /dashboard/cart-recovery-messages` | `cart_recovery_messages.html` вЂ” recovery message templates. |
| `GET /dashboard/widget-customization` | `widget_customization.html` вЂ” widget appearance. |
| Shared chrome | `templates/partials/dashboard_sidebar.html`, `templates/partials/recovery_dashboard_styles.html`. |

### 2.3 Exit Intent UI

- **V2:** **`cartflow_widget_triggers.js`** / **`cartflow_widget_flows.js`** (orchestration) with shell UI modules; duplicate open guards (e.g. **`[CF TRIGGER BLOCKED]`** paths) live in layered code. **Fast-add race recovery v1:** storefront bridge POST в†’ **`onStorefrontCartPersisted`**; deferred flush uses **`[CF TRIGGER DEFERRED REPLAY]`** (never silent drop when cart-event succeeds).
- **Legacy:** Implemented inside **`static/cartflow_widget.js`** when that file is the only widget bootstrap.

Server-side template control (**`exit_intent_*`** on **`Store`**): `services/store_template_control.py` merge through **`/api/recovery-settings`**.

### 2.4 Cart Recovery UI

- **Dashboard:** recovery settings + cart recovery messages pages above.
- **Widget (V2):** layered **Ui / Flows / Api** backed by **`/api/cartflow/*`** helpers above.
- **Widget (legacy):** reason capture, handoff, and preview in **`cartflow_widget.js`** (including **`/api/cart-recovery/reason`** where wired).

**How UI interacts with backend:** JSON `fetch` / XHR to FastAPI routes; dashboards use embedded scripts or `static/cartflow_dashboard_messages.js` for shared save/load patterns against **`/api/recovery-settings`**.

### 2.5 Brand / visual identity (official foundation v1)

| Asset | Role |
|--------|------|
| `branding/cartflow_brand_foundation_v1/` | **Official source of truth** вЂ” approved Visual Identity board: CF monogram logo, six-color green palette, Tajawal typography, process + dashboard icons, governance. Spec only until product UI migration. |
| `branding/cartflow_brand_system_v1.md` | Superseded historical spec (blue tokens) вЂ” do not use for new work. |
| `branding/_archive/logo_explorations/` | **Frozen** exploration archive (v1, v2, validation) вЂ” do not use in production. |

Product UI may still use legacy styling (landing green variants, widget purple `#6C5CE7`) until each surface is migrated per foundation guidelines.

---

## 3) Backend Layer

### 3.1 FastAPI structure

- **`main.py`** вЂ” Core app: mounts `static/`, registers routers, **`POST /api/cart-event`**, **`/api/recovery-settings`**, **`/api/conversion`**, webhooks, **`GET /dashboard`**, **demo / commerce sandbox** routes (see В§3.2.1), recovery sequence orchestration.
- **`routes/cartflow.py`** вЂ” `APIRouter(prefix="/api/cartflow")`: analytics, ready, public-config, generate-whatsapp-message, reason, etc.
- **`routes/knowledge.py`** вЂ” `APIRouter(prefix="/api/knowledge")`: **`GET /report`** вЂ” read-only evidence-based store insights (Knowledge Layer v1; merchant auth; no writes). **`GET /health`** вЂ” read-only Knowledge Layer health (`knowledge_health_v1.py`: coverage, confidence distribution, stale/missing inputs, diagnosis codes; product foundation bridge via `knowledge_product_metrics_v1.py` only). Metrics: honest purchase attribution (`knowledge_purchase_attribution_v1.py`); VIP isolated in `vip_evidence` bucket (`knowledge_metrics_v1.py`).
- **`routes/product_data.py`** вЂ” `APIRouter(prefix="/api/product-data")`: **`GET /health`** вЂ” read-only product data readiness (`services/product_data/product_data_health_v1.py`: payload coverage/name/id/variant rates, catalog flag, confidence, readiness classification; **additive** `payload_health`, `foundation_health` (`product_foundation_health_v1.py`: snapshot/catalog/hesitation/purchase mapping coverage from foundation tables), `identity_coverage` (`product_identity_coverage_v1.py`: lines capture rate, carts with/without lines, identity capture status); merchant auth; no writes). **Cart line snapshots v1:** immutable `cart_line_snapshots` rows from widget `lines[]` on `cart_state_sync` / `cart_abandoned` via `services/product_data/product_cart_snapshots_v1.py` + `product_data_line_snapshots_hook_v1.py` delegate in `main.py` (insert-only; dedup by content hash; no UI/API). **Catalog normalization v1:** mutable canonical `product_catalog_entries` via `product_catalog_v1.py` + `product_catalog_normalizer_v1.py` (identity tiers AвЂ“E; chained from same cart-event hook; reads snapshots / `lines[]` / `cf_product_catalog_json`; no UI). **Hesitation Mapping v1:** immutable `product_hesitation_mappings` (Product в†” Reason links) via `product_hesitation_mapping_v1.py` + `product_hesitation_types_v1.py`; non-blocking `product_hesitation_hook_v1.py` delegate fired from the reason-capture write path (`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`) вЂ” maps the captured `CartRecoveryReason` to canonical products present in the session (from cart line snapshots); insert-only, `dedup_hash` unique; read helpers only (`reasons_for_product`, `products_for_reason`, `mapping_count_for_store`); no intelligence/UI/API. **Purchase Mapping v1:** immutable `product_purchase_mappings` (Product в†” Purchase links) via `product_purchase_mapping_v1.py` + `product_purchase_types_v1.py`; non-blocking `product_purchase_hook_v1.py` delegate fired from Purchase Truth `record_purchase` (`services/cartflow_purchase_truth.py`) вЂ” maps canonical session products when purchase is confirmed; insert-only, `dedup_hash` unique; read helpers only (`purchases_for_product`, `products_for_purchase`, `purchase_mapping_count`); no intelligence/UI/API. **Governance v1:** read-only growth/query-cost/archive-policy diagnostics via `product_foundation_governance_v1.py` + related modules; `GET /api/product-data/governance/health` (merchant auth); no writes, archive jobs, or behavior changes to capture layers.
- **`routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`** вЂ” `APIRouter(prefix="/api/cart-recovery")`: **`POST /reason`** (widget reason persistence).
- **`routes/ops.py`** вЂ” **`GET /ping`**, **`GET /config-check`**, **`GET /decision-check`**, **`GET /health`**, **`GET /health/scheduler`**, dev mock-cart / set-token utilities.
- **`routes/public.py`** вЂ” **`GET /`** (landing), **`GET /register`** (302 в†’ `/signup`).
- **`routes/merchant_pages.py`** вЂ” dashboard **redirect** routes (Phase 1B) plus **shell/template** routes (Phase 1C): `GET /dashboard`, `/dashboard/analytics`, `/dashboard/exit-intent-settings`, `/dashboard/general-settings`, `/dashboard/test-widget`, and legacy redirects. **`GET /dashboard/normal-carts/operations`** remains on **`main.py`**.
- **`routes/dev_diagnostics.py`** вЂ” read-only **`GET /dev/*`** diagnostic routes (Phase 1D + 1E-A): route inventory, config/production-readiness reports, widget/store-identity/runtime truth, recovery/lifecycle/merchant-truth traces, **`GET /dev/snapshot-truth-diagnostics`** (alias-aware snapshot vs live-builder vs dashboard visibility), **`GET /dev/dashboard-builder-parity`** (full DB в†’ live builder в†’ snapshot builder в†’ persisted snapshot в†’ dashboard parity chain with `drop_stage` / `parity_status`; governance gate before visibility fixes), recovery-health, delay/attempts/unit verify, dashboard render test, recovery logs, test-widget identity trace, plus preview/timing-only routes (`/dev/run-flow`, `/dev/whatsapp-message-test`, `/dev/should-send-test`, `/dev/recovery-timing-test`, `/dev/recovery-duplicate-test`). Write/send/simulation/VIP/recovery-settings harness routes remain on **`main.py`**; **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`** middleware unchanged.
- **`routes/demo_panel.py`** вЂ” demo utilities.
- **`routes/merchant_auth.py`** вЂ” SaaS auth HTML: **`/login`**, **`/signup`**, **`/logout`**, **`/forgot-password`**, **`/reset-password`**; signed cookie session (`services/merchant_auth_http.py`); gate middleware on **`/dashboard*`** and **`/api/dashboard*`** (`ENV=development` demo bypass only).
- **`services/merchant_setup_unified_p0.py`** вЂ” **P0 unified setup:** one home card (`unified_p0`, `setup_mode`) вЂ” sandbox steps (account в†’ test-widget в†’ recovery в†’ carts в†’ verified) then unlocked production (store connect, WhatsApp, templates, live widget); composes **`evaluate_onboarding_readiness`** + **`merchant_activation_v1`** + **`merchant_onboarding_v1`** (no recovery/send changes). Daily KPIs hidden via **`ma-setup-mode`** until complete.
- **`services/merchant_onboarding_journey_v2.py`** вЂ” **Onboarding V2 UX:** 6-step activation checklist + progress bar + nav locks + readiness card (truth-derived checklist: widget, store, WhatsApp, recovery) + guided empty states on **`GET /api/dashboard/summary`** (`merchant_setup_experience.activation_journey_v2`); merchant SPA render in **`merchant_dashboard_lazy.js`** (no behavior engine changes). Hardening audit: **`docs/cartflow_onboarding_hardening_audit_v2.md`**, tests **`tests/test_merchant_onboarding_hardening_audit.py`**.
- **`services/merchant_onboarding_v1.py`** + **`merchant_setup_experience_v1`** + **`merchant_onboarding_store.py`** + **`merchant_store_connection_v1.py`** вЂ” guided onboarding (5 steps); Store resolved only from authenticated merchant session; **`/dashboard#settings`** store connection card (Zid OAuth when `ZID_CLIENT_*` configured, else В«Щ…ЩЉШІШ© Ш§Щ„Ш±ШЁШ· Щ‚ЩЉШЇ Ш§Щ„ШҐШ№ШЇШ§ШЇВ»); **`GET /api/merchant/store-connection`** (+ zid connect / disconnect). After Zid OAuth link, **`services/zid_storefront_widget_install_v1`** records widget install status (Partner Custom Snippet вЂ” no per-store install API); **`POST /api/storefront/widget-seen`** + loader beacon for **`widget_last_seen_at`**.
- **`services/merchant_activation_v1.py`** + **`merchant_dashboard_home_stage_v1.py`** вЂ” scoped activation demo; adaptive home stages (`activation` / `activated` / `production`) on **`GET /api/dashboard/summary`** (`merchant_activation.home_stage`); landing CTAs **`/signup`**.
- **`services/store_identity_v1.py`** + **`store_identity_aliases`** table вЂ” **canonical Store identity layer:** maps CartFlow `zid_store_id`, Zid permalink/numeric/uuid, future Salla ids, dashboard slugs, widget `public-config` keys, and recovery_key prefixes to one **`Store`** row via **`resolve_store_row_by_identifier`** (used by **`recovery_store_lookup`**, widget public API, OAuth sync, widget cache keys). No latest-Store fallback. **Warm hot path is offline:** `sync_connected_platform_identities()` makes **no live Zid network calls by default** (`warm_live_platform_sync_enabled()` / `CARTFLOW_WARM_LIVE_PLATFORM_SYNC=1` to opt in) вЂ” a blocking per-store Zid API call during request-time warm previously hung phone-capture / dashboard endpoints under the `db_warm` lock. Aliases are still backfilled offline from `Store` columns (`identity_backfill` stage) and refreshed at OAuth callback time.
- **`services/widget_configuration_trust_v1.py`** вЂ” **Widget Configuration Trust Recovery v1:** RC1вЂ“RC7 validation, dashboardв†”public-config parity, visibility diagnostics (`would_show_widget`, blockers), closure criteria; consumed by **`GET /api/admin/operations/widget-configuration-trust`** (admin JSON, no UI).
- **`services/storefront_runtime_truth_gate_v1.py`** вЂ” **storefront runtime truth gate:** after widget settings save, syncs aliases + warms cache, compares dashboard DB vs `public-config` vs last storefront beacon (`POST /api/storefront/widget-seen`); persists `widget_runtime_truth_status` on **`Store`**; Admin Operations alert **`widget_settings_mismatch`** when mismatch/unresolved.
- **`services/vip_dashboard_batch_v1.py`** вЂ” **VIP dashboard batch read v1:** `GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts` hot path вЂ” one VIP cart SELECT + bulk reasons + bulk recovery logs в†’ pure `vip_dashboard_row_contract()` (zero DB in projection). Optional `?debug_perf=1` metadata. Settings/other surfaces still use **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`**.

### 3.2 Routes (representative)

| Route | Module | Role |
|--------|--------|------|
| `GET`/`POST /login`, `/signup`, `GET /logout`, `/forgot-password`, `/reset-password` | `routes/merchant_auth.py` | Merchant account signup/login; PBKDF2 passwords; reset tokens via Resend (`RESEND_API_KEY`, `RESEND_FROM_EMAIL`) or dev log when `ENV=development` without key. |
| `POST /api/cart-event` | `main.py` | Cart events (`cart_abandoned`, conversion flags, etc.). Merchant test-widget contract (when `merchant_activation=1`): enforce authenticated `store_slug`, evaluate old lifecycle truth, auto-reset to fresh `session_id`/`cart_id`/`recovery_key` when identity is not reusable. |
| `GET` / `POST /api/recovery-settings` | `main.py` | Store recovery + template + widget + VIP threshold merge/persist. |
| `POST /api/conversion` | `main.py` | Marks session converted; stops recovery. |
| `POST /api/cart-recovery/reason` | `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py` | Upsert `CartRecoveryReason` (Layer D). |
| `GET /api/cartflow/*`, `POST /api/cartflow/*` | `routes/cartflow.py` | Readiness, mock messages, analytics. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/recovery-trend` | `main.py` | Dashboard chart data. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts` | `main.py` + `services/vip_dashboard_batch_v1.py` | VIP tab JSON вЂ” batch load (carts + reasons + logs) then pure projection; bounded SQL (в‰¤4 typical); `?debug_perf=1` for dev query/timing metadata. |
| `GET /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{cart_row_id}/manual-contact` | `main.py` | VIP ШЄЩ€Ш§ШµЩ„ ЩЉШЇЩ€ЩЉ Щ…Ш№ Ш§Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ вЂ” Щ‚Ш±Ш§ШЎШ© ЩЃЩ‚Ш·: `manual_contact_available` + `contact_href` ШЈЩ€ ШіШЁШЁ Ш№ШЇЩ… Ш§Щ„ШЄЩ€ЩЃШ± (Щ„Ш§ ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁ). |
| `POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{cart_row_id}/merchant-alert` | `main.py` | VIP Щ„Щ€Ш­Ш©: ШЄЩ†ШЁЩЉЩ‡ Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁ Щ„Щ„ШЄШ§Ш¬Ш± ЩЃЩ‚Ш· (`build_vip_merchant_alert_body` + `try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`Ш› `store_whatsapp_number` Ш«Щ… `whatsapp_support_url`). |
| `POST /api/carts/{id}/send` | `main.py` | ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ ЩЉШЇЩ€ЩЉ Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Ш№Щ„Щ‰ Ш§Щ„ШµЩЃШ­Ш© Ш§Щ„Ш±Ш¦ЩЉШіЩЉШ© Щ„Щ„Щ€Ш­Ш© (`send_whatsapp_message` Meta path) вЂ” **Щ„ЩЉШі Щ…ШіШ§Ш± VIP**. |
| `POST /dev/create-vip-test-cart` | `main.py` | Seed Ш­Щ‚ЩЉЩ‚ЩЉ: `AbandonedCart` VIP + `CartRecoveryReason` Ш¬Щ„ШіШ© `test_vip_session` ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† Щ€ШЇШ¬ШЄ (Щ…ШіЩ…Щ€Ш­ ЩЃЩЉ Ш§Щ„ШҐЩ†ШЄШ§Ш¬ Ш№ШЁШ± Щ‚Ш§Ш¦Щ…Ш© `_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`). |
| `GET /dev/widget-test`, `/dev/widget-test/cart` | `main.py` | **DEV-only legacy monolith harness** вЂ” HTML loads **`/static/cartflow_widget.js`** directly (no **`widget_loader`**, no **`cartflow_widget_runtime`**). **`no_dev_in_production`**: **`404`** unless **`ENV=development`**; intentionally **not** in **`_DEV_ROUTES_ALLOWED_WHEN_NOT_DEVELOPMENT`**. **`/demo/store`** remains **layered V2**. |
| `GET /dev/cartflow-simulation-report` | `main.py` + `services/cartflow_simulation_report_v1.py` | **Dry-run multi-store recovery simulation** for isolated **`sim-store-*`** slugs only (`stores=10` default, up to `100` with `expanded=true`). Runs 11 scenarios/store (cart, reason, 2-msg template, schedules, simulated sends, reply, return, purchase, dashboard truth). No WhatsApp/Twilio; `cleanup=true` purges simulation rows. |
| `POST /webhook/zid` | `main.py` | Zid webhook в†’ cart upsert + purchase truth ingest when order-paid detected (`zid_webhook_purchase_v2`). |
| `POST` / `GET /webhook/whatsapp` | `main.py` | Twilio / inbound hook stubs (`[WA REPLY]` logging). |
| `POST /webhook/whatsapp/status` | `routes/whatsapp_delivery_webhook.py` | Twilio status callbacks в†’ `whatsapp_delivery_truth_v1` (`[WA DELIVERY EVENT]` / `[WA DELIVERY TRUTH]`); no recovery execution. |
| `GET` / `POST /webhooks/meta/whatsapp` | `routes/meta_whatsapp_webhook.py` + `services/meta_whatsapp_webhook_v1.py` | Meta Cloud API webhook verify (`hub.challenge` when `META_WEBHOOK_VERIFY_TOKEN` matches) + inbound event ingest (delivered/read/inbound message); in-memory diagnostics only вЂ” **no recovery execution**. |
| `GET /admin/whatsapp-webhook` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | Admin HTML вЂ” last Meta webhook payload, delivered/read/inbound diagnostics + raw JSON. |
| `GET /admin/api/whatsapp-webhook/diagnostics` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | Admin JSON for Meta webhook diagnostics (session auth). |
| `GET /admin/support-diagnostics` | `routes/admin_ops.py` | Admin JSON: `build_admin_support_diagnostics` вЂ” What/Why/Action for support (session/store/recovery_key). |
| `GET /admin/support-diagnostics/ui` | `routes/admin_ops.py` | Admin HTML session/recovery lookup; reached from the **Support Diagnostics** page (`/admin/diagnostics`). |
| `GET /admin/operations` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Executive overview v3.5 (Action First Mode)** вЂ” Store Action Center expanded cards are **action-first**: Root Cause в†’ Recommended Action в†’ Verification, with Impact / Affected Signals / investigation hints in collapsed **Technical Context**. Priority queue (v3.4), root cause grouping (v3.3), production truth (v3.2). Presentation-only вЂ” no detection changes. |
| `GET /admin/operations/issues` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Current Issues** вЂ” operational alerts re-expressed in business language (`_build_current_issues`), one card per kind with Impact/Affected/Owner/Suggested Action/Verification. |
| `GET /admin/diagnostics` | `routes/admin_operations.py` | **Support Diagnostics** (support-only) вЂ” Recovery Resume Health card + collapsible В«ШЄЩЃШ§ШµЩЉЩ„ ШЄЩ‚Щ†ЩЉШ© (Щ„Щ„ШЇШ№Щ… ЩЃЩ‚Ш·)В» panels lazy-loading the Investigation/Analytics partials via `GET /admin/operations/section/investigation` and `/section/analytics`; quick links to operational-health, support-diagnostics/ui, control. |
| `GET /admin/operations/section/widget-health` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `widget_health_v1.py` | **Widget Health v1** (read-only), **UX V2 action-first**: lazy HTML partial on the operations overview вЂ” status summary в†’ Current Widget Issues cards (13 kinds; Problemв†’Impactв†’Whereв†’Suggested Actionв†’Verification + collapsed Technical Details) shown first; full per-store matrix (installed, public-config, beacon, identity, cart bridge, hesitation armed, shown, last error, last seen, status рџџў/рџџЎ/рџ”ґ) collapsed under В«Store DiagnosticsВ». UI-only filters: Store Type (real/test) + hide-healthy by default (logic in parent overview script). Parses beacon `runtime_truth.widget_health` additively; no truth-system duplication. |
| `GET /admin/operations/snapshot` | `routes/admin_operations.py` + `admin_operational_snapshot_v1.py` | Read-only JSON operational snapshot export (optional `?store_slug=`); admin session auth; no secrets. |

### 3.2.1 Demo commerce sandbox (v1) вЂ” reference

**Purpose:** One in-app вЂњrealistic lightweight storeвЂќ that exercises the **real** recovery pipeline (cart events, continuation, dashboard, offers/product intelligence when configured) without replacing production widget architecture.

| Piece | Location / behavior |
|--------|---------------------|
| **Catalog (data)** | **`services/demo_sandbox_catalog.py`** вЂ” `SANDBOX_PRODUCTS`, `SANDBOX_PRODUCT_ORDER`, PDP numbering (`SANDBOX_PRODUCT_KEY_BY_NUM`). Fields: `id`, `sku`, `name`, `price` / `unit_price`, `category`, **`normalized_category`**, **`product_family`** (per SKU), descriptions, `url` / `image` (picsum seeds), **`related_keys`**, **`cheaper_alternative_keys`**, **`available`**. **Rule-first only** (no AI): relationships are explicit lists on each SKU. |
| **URLs per store** | `product_demo_url(nav_base, key)` вЂ” `/demo/store/...` vs `/demo/store2/...` so `demo2` PDP links stay isolated. |
| **Merchant sync** | `merchant_catalog_for_intelligence_sync()` / `merchant_catalog_json_string()` вЂ” JSON shaped for **`product_catalog`** in **`/api/recovery-settings`** (paste in dashboard **Ш§Щ„Ш№Ш±Щ€Ш¶ Ш§Щ„Ш°ЩѓЩЉШ©** so intelligence and offers match real catalog rows). Rows may include **`normalized_category`** and **`product_family`** for cheaper-matching (see **`cartflow_product_intelligence.py`**). Template context: `demo_merchant_catalog_json`. |
| **Store UI** | **`templates/demo_store.html`** вЂ” grid from `demo_grid_rows`, `window.CF_DEMO_PRODUCTS` + `window.CF_DEMO_NAV_BASE` from server JSON; PDP with image + related links; cart **subtotal** + link to checkout; **checkout** page with **COD** button в†’ **`window.cartflowTriggerDemoConversion`** в†’ **`POST /api/conversion`** (`purchase_completed: true`), then local cart clear + client converted flag (same as demo panel). |
| **Demo panel** | **`static/cartflow_demo_panel.js`** вЂ” cart page only UI; **`cartflowStartDemoScenario`** seeds **`hp_pro`** first (premium headphones) to surface **cheaper-alternative** scenarios; **`cartflowTriggerDemoConversion`** exported for checkout page. |
| **Abandon payload shape** | Demo sends **`cart` as a JSON array** of line objects (`id`, `name`, `price`, `category`, вЂ¦). **`services/recovery_product_context.py`** `_first_line_items_list` accepts **`cart` as list** so product context / intelligence see line items. |
| **Tests** | `tests/test_demo_behavioral_navigation.py` (routes, checkout), `tests/test_cart_recovery_sequence_behavior.py`, `tests/test_recovery_product_context.py` (list-cart case). |

**Do not use the sandbox as:** a second application or a bypass of lifecycle, continuation, or dashboard settings вЂ” it is wired to the same APIs and session keys as the existing demo.

### 3.3 Services (`services/`)

| Area | Modules |
|------|---------|
| WhatsApp mode (Production Strategy P1 + Mode Selection V1) | `merchant_whatsapp_mode_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_visibility_v1.py` вЂ” `stores.whatsapp_mode` (`cartflow_managed` default / `merchant_whatsapp`); prominent Arabic mode cards on `#whatsapp`; Path B panel (Meta pairing + Embedded Signup + `#whatsapp-connect`); admin `/admin/whatsapp`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_mode_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp Dual Architecture V1 (design) | **Path A** `cartflow_managed` (CartFlow Shared WhatsApp) vs **Path B** `merchant_whatsapp` (Merchant-Owned) вЂ” independent readiness, diagnostics, onboarding, sending provider (adapter boundary), dashboard messaging; path switch preserves settings; recovery engine unchanged. Target modules: `whatsapp_dual_readiness_v1`, `whatsapp_path_router_v1`, path A/B presentation builders. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_dual_architecture_v1.md`. |
| WhatsApp Embedded Signup Foundation V1 | Path B one-click onboarding prep вЂ” readiness states (`not_started` / `pairing_required` / `connected` / `failed`); `merchant_whatsapp_embedded_signup_readiness_v1.py`; placeholder `#whatsapp-connect` + `/dashboard/whatsapp-connect`; read-only `whatsapp_embedded_signup` API block. No SDK/token exchange/send/recovery changes. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_embedded_signup_foundation_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_embedded_signup_readiness_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp template registry (Production Strategy P2) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_registry_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_reason_mapping_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_template_layer_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_template_visibility_v1.py` вЂ” canonical 11-key registry + locked reasonв†’template map; merchant edits content on `#trigger-templates` only; admin `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/templates` + `/store-templates`. | WhatsApp template execution policy (Production Strategy P3) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_execution_policy_v1.py` вЂ” read-only 3-stage execution model, stop/skip vocabulary, VIP lane rules, Managed sender internal controls; `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/execution-policy`. | WhatsApp template library & guardrails (Production Strategy P4) | `merchant_whatsapp_template_library_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_meta_policy_awareness_v1.py`, `merchant_whatsapp_timing_guardrails_v1.py`, `admin_whatsapp_template_library_visibility_v1.py` вЂ” versioned library, approval/fallback architecture, calm guidance, stage 2/3 timing clamps on trigger-template save; `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/template-library`. No Meta/send migration. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_strategy_phase4_template_library_meta_readiness_policy_guardrails_audit_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_template_library_phase4_v1.py`. |
| WhatsApp connection & readiness (Production Strategy P5) | `merchant_whatsapp_connection_readiness_v1.py`, enriched `merchant_whatsapp_readiness_ui.py` вЂ” canonical connection states, readiness dimensions, production-truth copy; merchant `#whatsapp` readiness card; admin `GET /api/admin/whatsapp/connection-readiness` (per-store includes `readiness_diagnostic_temp`). No Meta/send migration. **UX V2 (action-first):** `CONNECTION_STATE_ACTION_FIRST` + `build_action_first_card` drive a per-state title/next-action/single-CTA/outcome card (`action_first` in merchant API); engine/states/truth unchanged. **Merchant presentation V1/V2:** `merchant_whatsapp_readiness_presentation_v1.py` вЂ” completed journey shows В«ШЄЩ… ШҐЩѓЩ…Ш§Щ„ ШҐШ№ШЇШ§ШЇ Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁВ» + separate В«Ш­Ш§Щ„Ш© Ш§Щ„ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„В» (Meta Business Platform pairing CTA when production send not ready; В«Щ‚ЩЉШЇ Ш§Щ„ШЄШ¬Щ‡ЩЉШІ ШЁЩ€Ш§ШіШ·Ш© CartFlowВ» only for sandbox/ops gaps); strips diagnostic from merchant API. **Onboarding Journeys UI V1:** `merchant_whatsapp_onboarding_journeys_v1.py` вЂ” `stores.whatsapp_onboarding_journey` (4 merchant paths); journey selector + guidance on `#whatsapp`; CTA В«Ш§Ш®ШЄЩЉШ§Ш± Щ…ШіШ§Ш± Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁВ» / В«Щ…ШЄШ§ШЁШ№Ш© Ш§Щ„ШЄЩЃШ№ЩЉЩ„В» (in-progress only); completed в†’ В«ШЄШ№ШЇЩЉЩ„ ШҐШ№ШЇШ§ШЇШ§ШЄ Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁВ». **Journey Execution Layer V1:** `merchant_whatsapp_journey_execution_v1.py` вЂ” journey-specific actionable CTAs + `whatsapp_onboarding_journey_status` (`not_started`/`in_progress`/`completed`); progress UI; readiness/admin integration; reserved future Meta hooks (not implemented). Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_production_reality_phase1_journey_execution_layer_v1.md`. Tests: `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_journey_execution_v1.py`, `tests/test_merchant_whatsapp_readiness_final_merchant_ux_v1.py`. Doc: `docs/cartflow_whatsapp_onboarding_journeys_ui_v1.md`. Wired in `whatsapp_send.send_whatsapp` only (all recovery/VIP paths use this). |

Observability only вЂ” no widget/recovery/classification changes. |
| DB Ready deep trace (v1, Step 4A) | `db_ready_diag_v1.py`, `db_ready_operational_snapshot_v1.py`, `db_ready_admin_v1.py` вЂ” `[DB READY STAGE]` / `[DB READY LOCK]` on `_merchant_dashboard_db_ready()` + `_ensure_cartflow_api_db_warmed()` + `ensure_production_store_schema()` branches; per-stage `query_count` + `total_sql_ms`; durable singleton `DbReadyOperationalSnapshot`; Admin Operations lazy section **Dashboard Initialization (Request Health)** with healthy/slow/blocking thresholds (3s / 15s). Observability only вЂ” no optimization. |
| DB Ready query explosion isolation (v1, Step 4B.1) | Extends Step 4A: `[DB READY SUBSTAGE]` per internal schema helper (widget_schema column migrations, merchant_auth bootstrap, widget_install columns, identity backfill/sync, schema verifiers); `[DB READY TOP STAGES]` ranked by query count; snapshot `top_substages_json` + Admin panel sub-stage table. Diagnostics only. |
| DB Ready root-cause classification (v1, Step 4B.2) | `db_ready_stage_reason_v1.py` вЂ” read-only probes emit `reason=` on tracked stages (`widget_schema`, `identity_backfill`, `identity_backfill_register`, `production_schema`, `bootstrap_merchant_auth`); identity backfill row counters (`rows_scanned`, `rows_updated`, `rows_inserted`); snapshot `stage_classifications_json` + Admin **Why did this run?** table. Diagnostics only вЂ” no optimization. |
| DB Ready startup warm (v1, Step 4B.3) | `db_ready_startup_warm_v1.py` вЂ” non-blocking background `_ensure_cartflow_api_db_warmed(trace_source="startup")` at app startup; `[DB READY STARTUP WARM]` logs; refresh-state defers with partial token while warm runs; snapshot startup warm status + Admin **Startup warm** panel. Moves cold-start cost off user-facing requests when warm completes first. |
| DB Ready restart survival (v1, Step 4B.4вЂ“4B.5) | `db_ready_restart_survival_v1.py` вЂ” durable restart verification (protection-focused PASS/FAIL, timing classification, `used_safe_path`); `[RESTART SURVIVAL]` logs with `timing=` / `protected=` / `reason=`; Admin **Restart Survival Verification** card; alert `dashboard_restart_survival_failed`. Read-only вЂ” no warm/behavior changes. |

### 3.4 Database models

Defined in **`models.py`**; optional columns ensured at runtime via **`schema_widget.ensure_store_widget_schema`**.

---

## 4) Core Logic Layer (Hard-core)

### 4.1 Detection Logic (Layer B)

- **`config_system.py`** вЂ” `get_cartflow_config(store_slug=...)`: isolated defaults (`recovery_delay_minutes`, `max_recovery_attempts`, `whatsapp_recovery_enabled`, etc.). Documented in code as **Layer B** (no DB required).
- **`services/whatsapp_send.py`** вЂ” `_recovery_config(store)` merges Layer B with store slug via `get_cartflow_config` for delay / attempt gates inside **`should_send_whatsapp`**.

### 4.2 Reason Capture (Layer C / D)

- **Layer D (persistence)** вЂ” **`POST /api/cart-recovery/reason`** in `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py`: validates payload, upserts **`CartRecoveryReason`** (`store_slug`, `session_id`, `reason`, `sub_category`, `custom_text`, `customer_phone`, `user_rejected_help`, etc.).
- Widget stores session keys and posts **`reason_tag`** aligned with dashboard / templates (see layered sources and comments in **`cartflow_widget.js`**).

### 4.3 Persistence (Layer D)

- **`CartRecoveryReason`** вЂ” last reason per `(store_slug, session_id)`; drives `updated_at` / last activity for delay checks.
- **`CartRecoveryLog`** вЂ” append-only recovery attempts (`status`, `step`, `message`, вЂ¦); includes **`vip_manual_handling`** for VIP dashboard lines.
- **`RecoverySchedule`** вЂ” durable delayed-recovery jobs (`recovery_key`, `due_at`, `effective_delay_seconds`, `delay_source`, `context_json`); survives process restart; resumed on startup via **`services/recovery_restart_survival`**.
- **`AbandonedCart`** вЂ” `zid_cart_id`, `cart_value`, `vip_mode`, etc.; VIP threshold comparison uses **`_abandoned_cart_cart_value_for_recovery`** in `main.py`.
- **`Store`** вЂ” recovery delays, units, attempts, templates, `vip_cart_threshold`, WhatsApp fields.
- **`schema_widget.py`** вЂ” idempotent `ALTER TABLE` helpers so ORM matches SQLite/Postgres deployments.

### 4.4 Decision Engine (D.2)

- **`services/decision_engine.py`** вЂ” `decide_recovery_action(reason_tag, store=..., is_vip_cart_flag=False)`:
  - **Normal:** maps reason в†’ `action` + message via **`resolve_whatsapp_recovery_template_message`**Ш› ЩЉЩЏШ№Ш§ШЇ ШЈЩЉШ¶Ш§Щ‹ **`send_customer: true`** Щ€ **`send_merchant: false`**.
  - **VIP (`is_vip_cart_flag=True`):** Щ‚ШЁЩ„ ШЈЩЉ Щ…Щ†Ш·Щ‚ Щ‚Щ€Ш§Щ„ШЁ вЂ” ЩЉЩЏШ№Ш§ШЇ **`action: vip_manual_handling`**, **`message: ""`**, **`send_customer: false`**, **`send_merchant: true`** Щ…Ш№ ШіШ¬Щ„ **`[VIP OVERRIDE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[VIP FLOW STOPPED]`**, **`[VIP CUSTOMER BLOCKED]`**.
- **`main._vip_recovery_decision_layer(reason_tag, store)`** ЩЉШіШЄШЇШ№ЩЉ Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш­Ш±Щѓ Щ…Ш№ **`is_vip_cart_flag=True`** Ш№Щ†ШЇ Щ…ШіШ§Ш±Ш§ШЄ VIP ЩЃЩЉ `main.py`.
- **Production recovery text** ШҐЩ„Щ‰ Ш§Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ ЩЉЩ…Ш± ШєШ§Щ„ШЁШ§Щ‹ ШЁЩЂ **`reason_template_recovery.resolve_recovery_whatsapp_message_with_reason_templates`** ШЇШ§Ш®Щ„ **`main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**Ш› Щ…ШіШ§Ш± VIP ЩЉЩ€Щ‚ЩЃ Ш°Щ„Щѓ Щ‚ШЁЩ„ Ш§Щ„ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„.

### 4.5 WhatsApp Integration (D.3)

- **Customer recovery (Twilio):** **`send_whatsapp`** in `services/whatsapp_send.py` вЂ” called from **`main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`** after gates. Logs **`[WA SEND PATH]`**, **`[WA SENT]`**, **`[WA STATUS]`** when trace/env allows.
- **Customer manual / CTA:** **`send_whatsapp_message`** in `main.py` вЂ” Meta Graph interactive `cta_url` (**`/api/carts/{id}/send`**).
- **Gates:** **`_blocked_send_whatsapp_if_user_rejected_help`** prints **`[BLOCK WA - USER REJECTED HELP]`**; **`should_send_whatsapp`** implements quiet period vs `CartRecoveryReason.updated_at`.

### 4.6 Delay Logic

1. **`handle_cart_abandoned`** claims session (`_try_claim_recovery_session`), loads store, **VIP short-circuit** (see В§4.9), else may schedule **multi** or async **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned`**.
2. **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned_impl`** polls **`_reason_tag_for_session`**, then either **`_schedule_recovery_multi_slots`** or computes **`get_recovery_delay`** (`services/recovery_delay.py`) vs elapsed time, then **`asyncio.create_task(_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned(..., delay_seconds=remain))`**.
3. **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**: **ЩЃШ­Шµ VIP Щ‚ШЁЩ„ **`asyncio.sleep`**** (Ш®Ш±Ш¬ ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Щ€Щ„Ш§ Ш§Щ†ШЄШёШ§Ш±)ШЊ Ш«Щ… **`await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)`** в†’ dedupe в†’ conversion / user-rejected в†’ **ЩЃШ­Шµ VIP Ш«Ш§Щ†ЩЌ** ШЇЩЃШ§Ш№ЩЉЩ‹Ш§ в†’ Ш§Щ„Щ‚Щ€Ш§Щ„ШЁ Щ€**`should_send_whatsapp`** Щ€**`send_whatsapp`** Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Ш­ШіШЁ Ш§Щ„Щ…ШіШ§Ш±Ш§ШЄ ШєЩЉШ± Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш­ШёЩ€Ш±Ш©.

Print-style trace: **`[DELAY STARTED]`**, **`[DELAY WAITING]`**, **`[DELAY FINISHED]`**, **`[CARTFLOW DELAY CHECK]`**, **`[DELAY BLOCKED]`**, **`[DELAY CONFIG]`** (from `whatsapp_send`).

### 4.7 Multi-message logic

- **`services/recovery_multi_message.multi_message_slots_for_abandon(reason_tag, store)`** вЂ” reads **`Store.reason_templates_json`**; if enabled and multiple messages в†’ list of `{index, delay_seconds, text}`.
- **`main._schedule_recovery_multi_slots`** вЂ” one asyncio task per slot, each calling **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned`** with **`multi_slot_index`** / **`multi_message_text`**.
- Logs: **`[MULTI MESSAGE MODE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE SCHEDULED]`**, **`[MULTI WA SEND ATTEMPT]`**, **`[MULTI WA SEND RESULT]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE SENT]`**, **`[MULTI MESSAGE FAILED]`**, **`[RECOVERY FULLY COMPLETED]`**.

### 4.8 Per-reason system

- **`get_recovery_delay(reason_tag, store_config)`** вЂ” per-tag default seconds in `services/recovery_delay.py` (extendable via `store_config.recovery_delays` if passed).
- **Reason templates** вЂ” `reason_templates_json` + `reason_template_recovery` / `store_reason_templates` / `recovery_message_templates` control message body and whether WhatsApp is blocked for a reason.

### 4.9 VIP handling

- **Threshold:** **`Store.vip_cart_threshold`** (null в†’ VIP ignored); Щ…Ш¬Щ…Щ€Ш№ Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш© Щ…Щ† **`_abandoned_cart_cart_value_for_recovery`** / Ш§Щ„Ш­Щ…Щ€Щ„Ш© Щ…Щ‚Ш§ШЁЩ„ **`services/vip_cart.is_vip_cart(cart_total, store)`**. **`cart_value`** Щ…ЩЃЩ‚Щ€ШЇ в†’ Щ„Ш§ Ш§Ш№ШЄШЁШ§Ш± VIP ЩЃЩЉ Ш§Щ„ШҐШґШ§Ш±Ш© Ш§Щ„ШЈЩ€Щ„Щ‰Ш› ЩЉЩ…ЩѓЩ† Щ„Щ„Щ…Щ‡Ш§Щ… Ш§Щ„Щ„Ш§Ш­Щ‚Ш© ШҐШ№Ш§ШЇШ© Ш§Щ„ШЄЩ‚ЩЉЩЉЩ….
- **Щ„Щ€Ш­Ш© Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„ вЂ” Щ…ШіШ§Ш± Щ€Ш§Ш­ШЇ:** **`/dashboard/normal-carts`** ЩЉШіШЄШЁШ№ШЇ Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„ Ш­ЩЉШ« `cart_value >= vip_cart_threshold`Ш› **`/dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** ЩЉШ№Ш±Ш¶Щ‡Ш§ ЩЃЩ‚Ш· Ш№Щ†ШЇ Щ€Ш¬Щ€ШЇ Ш№ШЄШЁШ© ШµШ§Щ„Ш­Ш©. **`GET /api/dashboard/normal-carts`** ЩЉШ¶Щ…Щ‘ ШµЩЃЩ€ЩЃ **`AbandonedCart`** Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш±ШЄШЁШ·Ш© ШЁШіШ¬Щ„Ш§ШЄ **`sent_real`/`mock_sent`** Ш­ШЄЩ‰ Щ„Щ€ Ш®Ш§Ш±Ш¬ Ш­ШЇ **`last_seen_at`**ШЊ Щ€ЩЉЩЏШЁЩ‚ЩЉ Щ…Ш¬Щ…Щ€Ш№Ш§ШЄ В«Щ…ЩЏШ±ШіЩ„В» ЩЃЩЉ ШЄШЁЩ€ЩЉШЁ Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„ Ш§Щ„Щ†ШґШ·Ш© Ш­ШЄЩ‰ Щ†ШЄЩЉШ¬Ш© Щ†Щ‡Ш§Ш¦ЩЉШ© (ШґШ±Ш§ШЎ / ШҐЩЉЩ‚Ш§ЩЃ / Ш§ЩѓШЄЩ…Ш§Щ„ ШЄШіЩ„ШіЩ„). **Щ…Щ„ЩѓЩЉШ© Ш§Щ„Ш­Щ‚ЩЉЩ‚Ш© (Phase 2):** `customer_lifecycle_state` (Щ…Щ† `services/customer_lifecycle_states_v1`) Щ‡Щ€ Ш§Щ„Щ…ШµШЇШ± Ш§Щ„Щ€Ш­ЩЉШЇ Щ„ШґШ§Ш±Ш© Ш§Щ„Ш­Ш§Щ„Ш©ШЊ bucket Ш§Щ„ШЄШЁЩ€ЩЉШЁШЊ Ш§Щ„Ш№ШЇЩ‘Ш§ШЇШ§ШЄШЊ Щ€ШЄЩ…Щ€Ш¶Ш№ Ш§Щ„ШЈШ±ШґЩЃШ©Ш› `merchant_cart_row_classifier` ЩЉШЁЩ‚Щ‰ Ш·ШЁЩ‚Ш© Щ…ШґШЄЩ‚Ш©/ШЄЩ€Ш§ЩЃЩ‚ ШєЩЉШ± ШіЩ„Ш·Щ€ЩЉШ©ШЊ Щ€timeline ШЇЩ„ЩЉЩ„ ЩЃЩ‚Ш·. **Cart archive identity (V1):** `services/cart_action_identity_v1.py` вЂ” archive/reopen mutations use cart-specific keys only; `store_slug:session_id` session-only alias excluded from writes and from `merchant_archived` read on lifecycle attach. **Cart reopen semantics (V1 decision):** `docs/cartflow_cart_reopen_semantics_v1.md` вЂ” reopen = restore active merchant visibility, not recovery restart; forbidden for purchased truth. Doc: `docs/cartflow_cart_action_audit_v1.md`. Ш§Щ„ШЄШґШ®ЩЉШµ ЩЃЩЉ JSON Ш§Щ„ШЁШ·Ш§Щ‚Ш©: `cart_total`, `vip_threshold`, `is_vip_cart`, `operational_lane` (`normal` \| `vip`). **`vip_mode`** ЩЃЩЉ DB ЩЉШЁЩ‚Щ‰ Щ„Щ„Щ…ШІШ§Щ…Щ†Ш©/Ш§Щ„Ш§ШіШЄШ±Ш¬Ш§Ш№Ш› Ш§Щ„Ш№Ш±Ш¶ Щ€Ш§Щ„ЩЂ **`POST вЂ¦/merchant-alert`** Щ€**`вЂ¦/lifecycle`** ЩЉШ№ШЄЩ…ШЇЩ€Щ† **`is_vip_cart`** Ш№Щ„Щ‰ Ш§Щ„Ш№ШЄШЁШ©.
- **Щ…ШІШ§Щ…Щ†Ш© ЩЃЩ€Ш±ЩЉШ© ШЁШ№ШЇ Ш§Щ„ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„:** `GET /api/dashboard/refresh-state` ЩЉЩ‚ШЇЩ‘Щ… `merchant_dashboard_refresh_token` Щ…Щ† `CartRecoveryLog` (latest log + latest sent + sent total). `static/merchant_dashboard_lazy.js` ЩЉШ±Ш§Щ‚ШЁ Ш§Щ„ШЄЩ€ЩѓЩ† ЩѓЩ„ 5 Ш«Щ€Ш§Щ†ЩЌ (no-store) Щ€ЩЉШ№ЩЉШЇ Ш¬Щ„ШЁ `summary` + `normal-carts` + `messages` ЩЃЩ‚Ш· Ш№Щ†ШЇ ШЄШєЩЉЩ‘Ш± Ш§Щ„ШЄЩ€ЩѓЩ†ШЊ ШЁШ­ЩЉШ« Ш±ШіШ§Щ„Ш© recovery Ш¬ШЇЩЉШЇШ© ШЄШёЩ‡Ш± ЩЃЩ€Ш±Ш§Щ‹ ШЇЩ€Щ† hard refresh.
- **`#carts` empty-on-load (V1):** `merchant_dashboard_lazy.js` вЂ” Щ„Ш§ ЩЉШ№Ш±Ш¶ В«Щ„Ш§ ШЄЩ€Ш¬ШЇ ШіЩ„Ш§Щ„В» ШҐЩ„Ш§ ШЁШ№ШЇ `normalCartsIsConfirmedFullEmpty` (live fetchШЊ `fc.all===0` ШµШ±ЩЉШ­ШЊ ШєЩЉШ± snapshot/degraded)Ш› boot ЩЉШіШЄШЇШ№ЩЉ `ensureNormalCartsPageReady` Щ€ЩЉШ№ЩЉШЇ Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш­Ш§Щ€Щ„Ш© ШЇЩ€Щ† Ш§Щ„Ш§Ш№ШЄЩ…Ш§ШЇ Ш№Щ„Щ‰ `#completed`.
- **Filter bar persistence (V1):** `merchant_app.js` вЂ” Ш§Ш®ШЄЩЉШ§Ш± ШґШ±ЩЉШ· Ш§Щ„ШЄШµЩЃЩЉШ© (sent/attention/вЂ¦) ЩЉЩЏШ­ЩЃШё ЩЃЩЉ `sessionStorage` (`ma_normal_cart_filter_v1`) Щ€Щ„Ш§ ЩЉЩЏШіШЄШЁШЇЩ„ ШЁЩЂ `#carts?tab=all` Ш№Щ†ШЇ reapply ШЁШ№ШЇ refreshШ› В«Ш§Щ„ЩѓЩ„В» ШµШ±ЩЉШ­ ЩЃЩ‚Ш· Ш№ШЁШ± chip ШЈЩ€ `goToCartTab('all')`.
- **Ш·ШЁЩ‚Ш© Щ‚Ш±Ш§Ш± D.2:** **`_vip_recovery_decision_layer`** в†’ **`decide_recovery_action(..., is_vip_cart_flag=True)`**Ш› Щ„Ш§ ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Щ‚Щ€Ш§Щ„ШЁ Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Щ…Щ† Ш§Щ„Щ…Ш­Ш±Щѓ Ш№Щ†ШЇ Щ‡Ш°Ш§ Ш§Щ„Ш№Щ„Щ….
- **Activation:** **`main._activate_vip_manual_cart_handling`** ЩЉШ¶Ш№ **`vip_mode`**ШЊ **`CartRecoveryLog`** ШЁЩЂ **`status=vip_manual_handling`**ШЊ **`try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`** (Щ†Шµ: **`build_vip_merchant_alert_body`**Ш› Щ‡ШЇЩЃ: **`store_whatsapp_number`** Ш«Щ… **`whatsapp_support_url`** Ш§Щ„Щ‚Ш§ШЁЩ„ Щ„Щ„ШЄШ­Щ„ЩЉЩ„)ШЊ Щ€ЩЉШ¶ШЁШ· **`_session_recovery_sent`** Ш№Щ†ШЇ Ш§Щ„Щ†Ш¬Ш§Ш­ ШЈЩ€ Ш№Щ†ШЇ ЩѓШ§Щ† **`vip_mode`** Щ…ЩЃШ№Щ‘Щ„Ш§Щ‹ Щ…ШіШЁЩ‚Ш§Щ‹Ш› **`_mark_vip_customer_recovery_closed`** ЩЉЩ…Щ†Ш№ ШЈЩЉ ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Щ…ШЄШ§ШЁШ№Ш© Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Щ„Щ‡Ш°Щ‡ Ш§Щ„Ш¬Щ„ШіШ© ШЁШ№ШЇ Ш§Ш№ШЄШЁШ§Ш± Ш§Щ„ШіЩ„Ш© VIP ЩЃЩЉ **`handle_cart_abandoned`**.
- **ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Щ…Щ‡Щ…Ш§ ЩѓШ§Щ† ШЄЩЃШ№ЩЉЩ„ DB:** ШҐШ°Ш§ **`is_vip_cart`** ШµШ­ЩЉШ­Ш© ЩЃЩЉ **`handle_cart_abandoned`** ШЈЩ€ **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned_impl`** в†’ Щ„Ш§ ЩЉЩЏШ¬ШЇЩ€Щ„ **`multi`** Щ€Щ„Ш§ **`_run_recovery_sequence`** ЩѓЩ…ШіШ§Ш± Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„Ш› ЩЃШґЩ„ ШЄЩ…ЩЉЩЉШІ DB Щ„Ш§ ЩЉЩЃШ№Щ‘Щ„ **fallback** ШҐЩ„Щ‰ Ш§ШіШЄШ±ШЇШ§ШЇ Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ ШЈЩ€ШЄЩ€Щ…Ш§ШЄЩЉЩѓЩЉ. ЩЃЩЉ **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl`**: ЩЃШ­Шµ VIP **Щ‚ШЁЩ„ **`asyncio.sleep`**** Щ„Ш№ШЇЩ… ШЄШЈШ®ЩЉШ± VIPШ› ЩЃШ­Шµ Щ„Ш§Ш­Щ‚ ШЇЩЃШ§Ш№ЩЉ ШЁШ№ШЇ Ш§Щ„ШЄШЈШ®ЩЉШ± ЩЉЩ…Щ†Ш№ **`send_whatsapp`** Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„.
- **ШЄЩ†ШЁЩЉЩ‡ ШЄШ§Ш¬Ш± ШЄЩ„Щ‚Ш§Ш¦ЩЉ (VIP Ш¬ШЇЩЉШЇ):** ШЁШ№ШЇ **`cart_state_sync`** / **`cart_abandoned`** Ш№Щ†ШЇ ШЈЩ€Щ„ ШЇШ®Щ€Щ„ Ш§Щ„Щ…ШіШ§Ш± Ш§Щ„ШЄШґШєЩЉЩ„ЩЉ VIP вЂ” **`_vip_merchant_auto_alert_if_newly_entering`** в†’ **`_send_vip_merchant_auto_alert`** (ЩЉШ­ШЄШ±Щ… **`merchant_vip_notify_enabled`**Ш› ЩЉШЄШ®Ш·Щ‰ ШҐЩ† **`vip_notify_enabled=false`**). Ш§Щ„ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ **Щ…ШЄШІШ§Щ…Щ†** ШЁШ№ШЇ commit Щ…Ш№ **poll Twilio** (`poll_twilio_vip_alert_delivery_truth`). **`CartRecoveryLog`** ШЁЩЂ **`reason_tag=vip_merchant_alert`** + Ш­Ш§Щ„Ш© **`vip_merchant_alert_accepted|delivered|failed`** (Щ„ЩЉШі **`sent_real`**). **`resolve_vip_alert_destination`**: **`store_whatsapp_number`** в†’ **`whatsapp_support_url`** в†’ **`CARTFLOW_VIP_ALERT_DESTINATION`**. **`vip_operational_truth_v1`**: Ш§ШіШЄШЁШ№Ш§ШЇ ШЄЩ†ШЁЩЉЩ‡Ш§ШЄ Ш§Щ„ШЄШ§Ш¬Ш± Щ…Щ† **`sent_count`** / augment / follow-up clarity Ш№Щ„Щ‰ **`normal-carts`**. **`GET /dev/vip-merchant-alert-operational-truth`** ЩЉШ№Ш±Ш¶ **`delivery_truth`** + **`normalized_destination_phone`**. ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Ш§Щ„ШЄШ§Ш¬Ш± ЩЉШЄШ®Ш·Щ‰ ШЁЩ€Ш§ШЁШ© Щ‚Щ€Ш§Щ„ШЁ 24 ШіШ§Ш№Ш© (**`vip_merchant_alert`** ЩЃЩЉ **`_MERCHANT_ONLY_WA_REASON_TAGS`**).
- **Щ„Щ€Ш­Ш© VIP вЂ” Щ‚Ш§Ш¦Щ…Ш© Ш§Щ„ШЄШЁЩ€ЩЉШЁ:** **`GET /api/dashboard/vip-carts`** Ш№ШЁШ± **`build_vip_dashboard_api_payload`** вЂ” batch SELECT VIP carts + bulk reasons/logsШЊ Ш«Щ… **`vip_dashboard_row_contract`** (ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† N+1Ш› Щ„Ш§ **`db.session.get`** Щ€Щ„Ш§ **`_reason_tag_for_abandoned_cart`** ШЇШ§Ш®Щ„ Ш§Щ„Ш­Щ„Щ‚Ш©). **`GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** Щ€ШєЩЉШ±Щ‡Ш§ Щ…Ш§ ШІШ§Щ„ШЄ **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`**.
- **Щ„Щ€Ш­Ш© VIP вЂ” ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ ЩЉШЇЩ€ЩЉ:** **`POST /api/dashboard/vip-cart/{id}/merchant-alert`**Ш› ШіШ¬Щ„ **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`**Ш› Щ†ЩЃШі **`try_send_vip_merchant_whatsapp_alert`** Щ…Ш№ Ш±ШіШ§Щ„Ш© UX Ш№Ш±ШЁЩЉШ© (**`Щ„Ш§ ЩЉЩ€Ш¬ШЇ Ш±Щ‚Щ… Щ€Ш§ШЄШіШ§ШЁ Щ„Щ„Щ…ШЄШ¬Ш±`** Ш№Щ†ШЇ Ш§Щ†Ш№ШЇШ§Щ… Ш§Щ„Ш±Щ‚Щ…).
- **Ш§Ш®ШЄШЁШ§Ш± ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† Щ€ШЇШ¬ШЄ:** **`POST /dev/create-vip-test-cart`** ЩЉЩ†ШґШ¦ **`AbandonedCart`** Ш«Ш§ШЁШЄ `zid_cart_id=vip-codegen-test-cart-1` (**`cart_value=1200`**, **`vip_mode=true`**, **`status=abandoned`**) + **`CartRecoveryReason`** (**`session_id=test_vip_session`**, **`reason=price`**); ЩЉШЁЩЉЩ‘Щ† ЩЃЩЉ Щ‚Ш§Ш¦Щ…Ш© ШЈЩ€Щ„Щ€ЩЉШ© VIP Ш№Щ†ШЇ **`interactive`** Ш­Щ‚ЩЉЩ‚ЩЉШ©.
- **Logs (Ш¬ШІШЎ):** **`[VIP CHECK]`**, **`[VIP MODE ACTIVATED]`**, **`[VIP CUSTOMER RECOVERY SKIPPED]`**, **`[VIP ACTIVATION FAILED]`**, **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT ATTEMPT]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT SENT]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED] reason=вЂ¦`** (**`vip_merchant_alert.py`**).

---

## 5) End-to-End Flow

**Widget в†’ Backend в†’ Decision в†’ Delay в†’ WhatsApp в†’ Dashboard**

1. User interacts with the layered **V2** runtime (`cartflow_widget_runtime/**`) or legacy **`cartflow_widget.js`** on the storefront; reason persistence follows the active surface (`/api/cartflow/reason` vs `/api/cart-recovery/reason`) в†’ row in **`cart_recovery_reasons`** when applicable.
2. Store platform (or demo) sends **`POST /api/cart-event`** with `event: cart_abandoned`, `store`, `session_id`, optional `cart_id` / `phone`.
3. **`handle_cart_abandoned`**: conversion / duplicate / claim checks в†’ load **`Store`** в†’ **ШҐШ°Ш§ VIP** (`is_vip_cart`): Ш§ШіШЄШЇШ№Ш§ШЎ **`_vip_recovery_decision_layer`** Ш«Щ… **`_activate_vip_manual_cart_handling`** Ш«Щ… **`_mark_vip_customer_recovery_closed`** Щ€**`return`** (Щ„Ш§ Ш¬ШЇЩ€Щ„Ш© ШҐШ±ШіШ§Щ„ Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ Ш­ШЄЩ‰ Щ„Щ€ ЩЃШґЩ„ Ш¬ШІШЎ Ш§Щ„ШЄЩЃШ№ЩЉЩ„).
4. If **multi_message_slots_for_abandon** returns slots в†’ schedule delayed tasks per slot; else **`_run_recovery_dispatch_cart_abandoned`** waits for reason if needed, then schedules **one** delayed **`_run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned`**.
5. After sleep (ШєЩЉШ± Щ…ШіШ§Ш± VIP Ш§Щ„Щ…ШЄЩ€Щ‚Щ‘ЩЋЩЃ Щ…ШіШЁЩ‚Ш§Щ‹): **VIP guard** ШЇЩЃШ§Ш№ЩЉШ› Ш«Щ… Ш±ШіШ§Ш¦Щ„ Ш§Щ„Щ‚Щ€Ш§Щ„ШЁ Щ€**`should_send_whatsapp`** Щ€**`send_whatsapp`** Щ„Щ„Ш№Щ…ЩЉЩ„ ЩЃЩ‚Ш· Ш®Ш§Ш±Ш¬ VIP.
6. **`_persist_cart_recovery_log`** records queued / sent / skipped / VIP rows.
7. **Dashboard** **`GET /dashboard`** вЂ” KPIs Щ€ШЈШіШЁШ§ШЁ Щ€Щ†ШґШ§Ш· Щ…Щ† **`AbandonedCart`** / **`CartRecoveryReason`** ЩЃЩ‚Ш·. **Щ‚Ш§Ш¦Щ…Ш© ШЈЩ€Щ„Щ€ЩЉШ© VIP** ЩЃЩЉ **`GET /dashboard/vip-cart-settings`** Ш№ШЁШ± **`_vip_priority_cart_alert_list()`** (Ш§Щ„Ш§ШіЩ… **`_vip_cart_alerts_merchant_list()`** alias Щ„Щ„ШЄЩ€Ш§ЩЃЩ‚Ш› ШЁШЇЩ€Щ† ШЄЩѓШ±Ш§Ш± ЩЃЩЉ Ш§Щ„Ш±Ш¦ЩЉШіЩЉШ©).

---

## 6) Data Models

### `MerchantUser` / auth (`merchant_users`, `merchant_password_reset_tokens`)

`MerchantUser`: `email`, `password_hash`, `merchant_name`, `primary_store_id`. Signup creates a **`Store`** row and sets **`stores.merchant_user_id`** + **`primary_store_id`** (startup DDL via `schema_merchant_auth`); orphan accounts without a store can complete signup with the same email/password. **`POST /signup`** logs **`[SIGNUP 400]`** on validation/register failure. Password reset tokens stored hashed with expiry.

### `Store` (`stores`)

Recovery: `recovery_delay`, `recovery_delay_unit`, `recovery_attempts`, `recovery_delay_minutes`. Optional **`merchant_user_id`** (FK) for SaaS ownership. WhatsApp / UX: `whatsapp_support_url`, `store_whatsapp_number`, `whatsapp_recovery_enabled`, `whatsapp_provider_mode` (merchant dashboard v1 вЂ” display/persist; send runtime still uses `config_system` gates), per-reason templates. **VIP (merchant prefs v1):** `vip_enabled`, `vip_notify_enabled`, `vip_note` (display/persist only); **`vip_cart_threshold`** still drives operational lane via `is_vip_cart` / `merchant_vip_threshold_int` (`template_*`, `trigger_templates_json`, `reason_templates_json`), `template_mode` / `tone` / `template_custom_text`, exit intent fields, widget customization (`widget_name`, `widget_primary_color`, `widget_style`). **VIP:** `vip_cart_threshold`.

### `AbandonedCart` (`abandoned_carts`)

`zid_cart_id`, `cart_value`, `status`, URLs, timestamps, **`vip_mode`**, `raw_payload`, optional `store_id`.

### Recovery-related

- **`CartRecoveryReason`** вЂ” last widget reason + phones + rejection flags.
- **`CartRecoveryLog`** вЂ” recovery audit trail (`status`, `step`, `message`, вЂ¦); statuses include **`vip_manual_handling`**, **`mock_sent`**, **`skipped_*`**, **`stopped_converted`**, etc.
- **`AbandonmentReasonLog`**, **`ObjectionTrack`**, **`RecoveryEvent`**, **`MessageLog`** вЂ” ancillary tracking / webhooks / messaging history as used across routes and webhooks.

---

## 7) Logs & Debugging

| Log / prefix | Where |
|----------------|--------|
| `[CF API]` | `main.handle_cart_abandoned` / cart-event |
| `[VIP OVERRIDE ACTIVATED]`, `[VIP FLOW STOPPED]`, `[VIP CUSTOMER BLOCKED]` | `services/decision_engine.py` (Ш№Щ†ШЇ `is_vip_cart_flag`) |
| `[VIP CHECK]`, `[VIP MODE ACTIVATED]`, `[VIP CUSTOMER RECOVERY SKIPPED]`, `[VIP ACTIVATION FAILED]`, **`[VIP MANUAL SEND CLICKED]`** | `main.py` |
| `[VIP MERCHANT ALERT ATTEMPT]`, `[VIP MERCHANT ALERT SENT]`, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT TRUTH]`**, **`[VIP MERCHANT AUTO ALERT SENT|SKIPPED|FAILED]`** | `services/vip_merchant_alert.py`, `main._send_vip_merchant_auto_alert` |
| `[DELAY STARTED]`, `[DELAY WAITING]`, `[DELAY FINISHED]`, `[DELAY BLOCKED]` | `main._run_recovery_sequence_after_cart_abandoned_impl` |
| `[CARTFLOW DELAY CHECK]`, `[CARTFLOW PRO LOGIC]` | `main.py` |
| `[DELAY CONFIG]` | `services/whatsapp_send.py` |
| `[MULTI MESSAGE *]` | `main.py` |
| `[WA SEND PATH]`, `[WA SEND REASON]`, вЂ¦ | `services/whatsapp_send.emit_recovery_wa_send_trace` |
| `[WA SENT]`, `[WA STATUS]` | `services/whatsapp_send.send_whatsapp` |
| `[BLOCK WA - USER REJECTED HELP]` | `services/whatsapp_send.py` |
| `[SKIP WA - USER REJECTED HELP]`, `[SKIP WA - MISSING REASON_TAG]`, `[SKIP WA - MISSING LAST_ACTIVITY]` | `main.py` |
| `[PHONE RESOLUTION]` | `main._log_phone_resolution` |
| `[WA SENDER MODE]` | `main.resolve_whatsapp_sender` |
| `[PHONE ATTACHED]` | `routes/cart_recovery_reason.py` |
| `[WA REPLY]`, `[WA FROM]` | `main` webhook/whatsapp |
| `[RECOVERY TASK EXIT CLEANLY]`, `[RECOVERY TASK CAUGHT ERROR]`, `[RECOVERY DISPATCH *]` | `main.py` |
| `[ANTI SPAM CHECK]`, `[ATTEMPT CONTROL]`, `[ATTEMPT BLOCKED]`, `[NO VERIFIED PHONE]` | `main.py` |
| `[WHATSAPP TEST]` | `main` dev endpoint |

---

## 8) Known Limitations

- **Two WhatsApp stacks:** Twilio (`send_whatsapp`) for scheduled recovery vs Meta Cloud (`send_whatsapp_message`) for manual cart send вЂ” different configuration and behavior.
- **Layer B vs DB:** `config_system` defaults apply when store-specific DB fields are null; merchants must align dashboard **Store** rows and migrations.
- **VIP merchant alert:** depends on **`store_whatsapp_number`** or parsable **`whatsapp_support_url`**, **`vip_notify_enabled`**, and Twilio config; otherwise skip/fail with **`[VIP MERCHANT AUTO ALERT SKIPPED]`** or **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT FAILED]`**. Dashboard **`merchant_vip_alert_state_ar`** is a count badge only вЂ” delivery truth is **`CartRecoveryLog`** (`vip_merchant_alert`) + **`[VIP MERCHANT ALERT TRUTH]`**.
- **`/webhook/whatsapp`:** minimal handler (prints body); not a full inbound conversation engine.
- **Schema drift:** legacy SQLite DBs need **`schema_widget.ensure_store_widget_schema`** (called from critical paths) so new ORM columns exist.
- **Dual widget bundles:** **default** merchant embed loads **V2** only; **`cartflow_widget.js`** is **explicit rollback** (**`__CARTFLOW_ALLOW_LEGACY_WIDGET`**) or **dev harness** вЂ” not the default **`widget_loader`** outcome. **`cartflow_widget.js`** remains large; contributors and **operational tests** still grep **`/api/`** / static markers in **both** trees.

---
